SELECT "s"."Id", "s"."Name", "t"."Id", "t"."Day", "t"."Duration", "t"."LectureTheatreId", "t"."SubjectId", "t"."Time", "t"."Id0", "t"."Capacity", "t"."Name"
FROM "Subjects" AS "s"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT "l"."Id", "l"."Day", "l"."Duration", "l"."LectureTheatreId", "l"."SubjectId", "l"."Time", "l0"."Id" AS "Id0", "l0"."Capacity", "l0"."Name"
    FROM "Lectures" AS "l"
    INNER JOIN "LectureTheatres" AS "l0" ON "l"."LectureTheatreId" = "l0"."Id"
) AS "t" ON "s"."Id" = "t"."SubjectId"
ORDER BY "s"."Id", "t"."Id"
